TS:
function $mol_guid(
    length = 8,
    exists: ( id: string )=> boolean = ()=> false,
) {

    for(;;) {

        let id = Math.random().toString( 36 ).substring( 2, length + 2 ).toUpperCase()
        if( exists( id ) ) continue
        return id
    }
}


JS:
function mol_guid(length = 8, exists = () => false) {
    while (true) {
        let id = Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, length + 2).toUpperCase();
        if (exists(id)) continue;
        return id;
    }
}

/// Division of any type
auto div( Num )( Num a, Num b ) {
    if( b == Num.init ) return Num.init;
    return a / b;
}

/// Division int:
unittest {
    assert( div( 6L, 3L ) == 2L );
}

/// Division floats:
unittest {
    assert( div( 6F, 3F ) == 2F );
}

/// Division by zero is safe:
unittest {
    assert( div( 0L, 0L ) == 0L );
}


–ì–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—Å—è —Ç–∞–∫–∞—è –¥–æ–∫–∞:

Comparison of client-side database management systems PGLite and $mol_db.

Results
          $mol_db  PGLite
lib-size  2.3 KB   3.9 MB
init      71 ms    2516 ms
insert    1.25 ms  92 ms
select    0.43 ms  83 ms
db-size   1 KB      2 MB


- $mol_db ~1700x smaller.
- $mol_db >70x faster.

Notice

- PGLite provides much more features.
- $mol_db doesn't allow SQL-Injections - no escaping required.
- $mol_db doesn't allow non-effective queries - only using indexes.
